The car was towed in for a no start/ clutch not working issue, you notified us the clutch was not in working order, and that the car was sitting for quite some time hence the no start issue. The first issue we found on your car is that the clutch was bound up, and the clutch pedal was stuck about half way down. Your car is equipped with a clutch safety switch, you have to fully press the clutch pedal down to activate this switch so it will allow the car to turn over to start. Since we couldn't force the pedal down we couldn't start the car, and if we bypassed the switch it would push forward because the clutch wouldn't disengage\n\nSo we went ahead and removed the the transmission to see what failed. We found that the  Throw-out bearing came apart. The clutch disc was down to the rivets, and the flywheel and pressure plate had serve heat spots. This is why we recommended a clutch kit. After replacing those parts we could continue the diagnostic for the no start, which the battery was no good, so we tried to charge it over night and it wouldn't hold a charge. So we installed a new battery. After failed attempts of starting it we went back to the basics and did a compression test, found that ALL 4 cylinders had 0psi. It would take further tear down to figure out why it has 0 compression.\n\nWe did try and find you a used engine, but they are quite pricey for your car, you have the type S which is the k20z1 a 2005-2006 only year engine. <name>Mik Hamilton<//name>< Time>
1402176946161</Time>
< Rate>
5<//Rate>
< Review>
They just opened...OK I'll be the first to review. I'm not sure whether to say I am an ice cream fanatic or and ice cream connoisseur. I love ice cream but I won't just eat ANY ice cream. I only want the best. I didn't know that they made ice cream "to order" when I entered. I loved the dairy laboratory looking atmosphere. There is a giant take of liquid nitrogen in the front which is how they freeze your ice cream to order. First I thought...ow wow this is probabably a good gimmick. I don't know if it is the ingredients or the freshness or a combination of the two but it was some of the best ice cream I have ever eaten. The texture was perfect and the vanilla flavor was just the right amount. They had only four flavor that day and I don't know if that it the plan of if they will expand the menu later. The small vanilla cup was $4.75 but it was generous (4) ounces). The pint costs $11. Pricey but worth it. Good luck on the new opening.</Review>

< text>
This is mixed bag for me. I'm giving it a four because the ice cream I ate was delicious. But was it "the freshest" or more delicious than other ice cream that isn't pumped out of the ceiling on demand? In my opinion, no. Because of this high maintenance process they only offer a small handful of flavors at once and the price is very high. To be honest it really did irratate me that you can't taste a thing before purchasing and that they had a sign up for a flavor that hadn't "been ready" all day.
For people who like futuristic tech and very cold ice cream.
Not for people who want some normal ice cream and I wouldn't recommend it for kids.</text>

<time>1465486169885< /time><review>Hi guys, I just wanted to review two of your products I have on my 2005 G35 sedan. (Very positive).
Your nismo style rear lip and nismo style side skirts were a dream to install. It took me 30 minutes or less to swap the side skirts over. They fit better than the OEM ones, using OEM hardware. They also provide more clearance for jacks and jack stands than the OEM ones did. Outstanding.
Installing your rear lip was also surprisingly easy. I used speed nut style hardware that bit into the OEM plastic bumper from underneath with 1/4-20 stainless hardware. No double sided tape needed. The result was a removable, steadily mounted lip with tight body lines thanks to your mold design.
You guys changed my mind about fiberglass products. Your parts do not feel brittle and ready to crack at any moment, they are flexible and sturdy.

<name>Dan Schimpf< /name>< Text>
Was traveling from Sacramento to Yuma Arizona and my 2017 RAM 2500 Laramie Limited started to develop a vibration that seemed to be coming from the rear end area.  I thought I was losing a u-joint in the rear driveline. I didn't want to be broke down somewhere along the highway in the middle of nowhere.
I pulled off of the freeway and stopped at Haddad Dodge without an appointment.
Explained my issue to one of the service writers and they immediately got a technician to do a test drive with me.
Due to the road surface on the freeway close to the dealership we couldn't exactly duplicate the issue. But he did feel the vibration.
We agreed that it could be a tire problem, driveline, or possibly something altogether different.
We agreed to start with doing a 4 tire balance and multipoint inspection.
They got me squeezed in between their other scheduled appointments and had me back on the road in a little over 4 hours.
It didn't fix my problem with the truck but I was at least reassured it wasn't the driveline.
Made it to Yuma without any problems.
Going to a tire shop tomorrow to have the tires throughly checked.
I would recommend Haddad Dodge and was very pleased with the service I received.<//Text>

After 2+ weeks, they finally said they didn't know when a DVD player would arrive and gave me back my van stating they "couldn't duplicate" anything. They blamed the service writer for bad writing/explanation of the problems. Though I did give them a hand-written list of the problems and obviously, they could've contacted me for further information.

Since they'd already ordered the DVD and FINALLY got it in...over a month later, I gave them the benefit of the doubt  and took it back in in March to get the DVD player replaced,  other previous issues, plus transmission issue looked at. They stated they rebuilt the transmission and swapped the DVD player. Their technician drove the vehicle over 300 miles (had 7/8 tank of gas when dropped off...light came on as soon as I left the dealership when I picked it up) "to get the radio to mess up". They supposedly did an update and once again "couldn't duplicate issues" with other concerns. But stated, "if it keeps happening, they'll have an engineer come look at it". WHY wouldn't they have contacted the engineer the second time it was there? The visit was planned well in advance because we live an hour away and have to take 2 vehicles to drop it off, work around work schedules, etc.

After we got it back the second time, we contacted the dealership because the rotors suddenly shook violently, which did not happen at all before taking it to them. Also, after the transmission work, my vehicle lost it's power to "take off" and is lagging and the fuel mileage has decreased. Also since they worked on it, my cruise control hasn't worked well, not keeping speed...either dropping over 5mph before engaging or not attempting to engine break at all.

We contacted the dealership multiple times, finally was passed through to Jeff, the customer service manager and told him the problems...he assured us he'd call back soon...3 weeks later we contacted him again and he always acted like he was unfamiliar with the vehicle/us. It makes me believe they have constant problems that a customer with two visits and a list of things not fixed doesn't ring a bell.

I explained my disgust that none of the issues were fixed and it came back with more than before it was taken to them. I asked him why it would take 3 times to bring in a vehicle before contacting the engineer and he said it could be MONTHS before a DODGE certified engineer could come...once again...why not have scheduled it before?

He denied this as a possibility and stated  they're "not a gas station". The service manager informed me "if the check engine light doesn't come on, then nothing is wrong with the vehicle". FALSE.

The service manager refused to tell me his qualifications when I asked considering his comments about the fuel pump/filter damage and cruise control.

She disappears into the service bay without so much as a by your leave, wanders out the back side, doesn't reappear for several minutes, strolls back in, has a 3 minute chat with one of the employees, disappears for another several minutes, then finally returns and informs me that the cost to repair my problem would be $290. I had already purchased a new switch module from an after market supplier. <Review>I purchased a Dodge Ram 2500 Long Horn from Haddad Dodge and up until recently was very satisfied with the truck.  After the last service we will not be coming back.  I called to make an appointment for routine maintenance, two recall items, and a couple of minor items that needed to be fixed.    The appointment was made several weeks and I was told to bring the truck in early so everything could be done in one day.  We live 70 miles away.

I brought the truck in on Thursday, 1-23-14.  They said it should be done by 3 or 4 pm.  I was given a car per my contract.  Around 5 pm I went back to the dealer to see what was going on and was told they would need to keep it another day to finish all the items.  Sure wish they would have called so I could have gone home earlier.  Next day I called around noon, since no one had called me.  They said it should be done by 2 pm.  Left my house at 1 and arrived at the dealer a little after 2.  I was told it was not done and give them until 4 to finish.  Waited for the call but it never came...went back to the dealer at 5 and was told it was just about ready.  They told me to return the rental and when I got back it would be done.  After getting the rental car checked in they called (hey...phone does work) and told me to keep the car because my truck was not ready.  I went back to the dealer and he said there was another page they had not seen and none of that work was done yet.  Also he told me they had called the warranty company and the left side windshield washer nozzle were not covered by the extended warranty because they were cosmetic; it does not function properly.

This really upset me because I was told the extended warranty that I purchased from the dealer at the time of the sale had the same coverage as the initial warranty.  I do not have the technical expertise to evaluate a warranty contract and so have to place my trust in the dealership; a mistake I will not make again.  It's ironic because the right side nozzle did the same thing and was replaced by them under warranty six months before.  The left side broke a month later (at about 35K miles) but I figured I would wait until the next scheduled service to get it fixed since I had the extended warranty.  We go to Bakersfield a couple times a month so I could have had it fixed under warranty had I known it would not be covered.

So I was told my truck would be ready on Monday or Tuesday.  Did not hear from anyone so I called on Tuesday and was told it was ready to go.  Let me be clear that I understand extra time will be necessary when unexpected problems come up.  However, there were no issues of that nature in this incident.  The only work done was what was scheduled;  less actually.  Five days to complete what I was told could be done in one.

There was a thick layer of dust over the entire interior;  not sure how so much dust could have got in there unless it was left with the windows open outside.  I went into the service office to tell them but several people were in line and a car was honking for me to move so I just left figuring what's the point; not like I'm coming back anyway.

Some may say I should not have a problem with the time issue because I had a "free" car.  However, I purchased a top of the line truck, not an entry level stripped to the bone car. I know they are busy; but a 1 minute call could have saved me hours. I am fairly meticulous about keeping my truck clean.  I expect it to get a little dirty during service but this thick layer of dust was unfathomable.

The issue on the extended warranty, the total disregard for my personal time by the service staff, and the condition of my truck when it was returned to me is beyond my tolerance so we will not be returning to this dealership.</Review>< Pics>
